<h1 _ngcontent-iri-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="Navigation"> Navigation </h1>

<div _ngcontent-iri-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>Navigation组件是路由导航的根视图容器，一般作为Page页面的根容器使用，其内部默认包含了标题栏、内容区和工具栏，其中内容区默认首页显示导航内容（Navigation的子组件）或非首页显示（<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navdestination">NavDestination</a>的子组件），首页和非首页通过路由进行切换。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>        <p>该组件从API version 8开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p></li>       <li>        <p>该组件从API version 11开始默认支持安全区避让特性(默认值为：expandSafeArea([SafeAreaType.SYSTEM, SafeAreaType.KEYBOARD, SafeAreaType.CUTOUT], [SafeAreaEdge.TOP, SafeAreaEdge.BOTTOM]))，开发者可以重写该属性覆盖默认行为，API version 11之前的版本需配合<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-expand-safe-area">expandSafeArea</a>属性实现安全区避让。</p></li>       <li>        <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navbar12">NavBar</a>嵌套使用Navigation时，内层Navigation的生命周期不和外层Navigation以及<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-modal-transition">全模态</a>的生命周期进行联动。</p></li>       <li>        <p>Navigation未设置主副标题并且没有返回键时，不显示标题栏。</p></li>       <li>        <p>Navigation的子页面切换时，新页面会主动请求焦点。</p></li>       <li>        <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-custom-component-lifecycle#abouttoappear">aboutToAppear</a>里面不建议使用栈操作。</p></li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 278px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>可以包含子组件。</p>     <p>从API version 9开始，推荐与<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navrouter">NavRouter</a>组件搭配使用。</p>     <p>从API version 10开始，推荐使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathstack10">NavPathStack</a>配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navdestination10">navDestination</a>属性进行页面路由。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 146px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 302px;">     <h3 id="navigation-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">Navigation<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navigation-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Navigation()</p>     <p>创建路由导航的根视图容器，适用于使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navrouter">NavRouter</a>组件进行页面路由。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 469px;">     <h3 id="navigation10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Navigation<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navigation10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Navigation(pathInfos: NavPathStack)</p>     <p>绑定导航控制器到Navigation组件，适用于使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathstack10">NavPathStack</a>配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navdestination10">navDestination</a>属性进行页面路由。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">pathInfos</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathstack10">NavPathStack</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">导航控制器对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 694px;">     <h3 id="navigation20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Navigation<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navigation20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Navigation(pathInfos: NavPathStack, homeDestination: HomePathInfo)</p>     <p>绑定路由栈到Navigation组件，并且指定一个NavDestination作为Navigation的导航栏（主页），适用于使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathstack10">NavPathStack</a>配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navdestination10">navDestination</a>属性或者系统路由表进行页面路由。使用示例参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#示例16navigation使用navdestination作为导航栏">示例16（Navigation使用NavDestination作为导航栏）</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">pathInfos</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathstack10">NavPathStack</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">路由栈信息。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">homeDestination</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#homepathinfo20">HomePathInfo</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">主页NavDestination信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>如果使用了主页NavDestination，则Navigation有如下变化：</p>       <ul>        <li>         <p>开发者写在Navigation组件内的内容不会被创建。</p></li>        <li>         <p>对于Navigation的各种属性，如果主页NavDestination有对应功能的属性，则Navigation的属性不生效。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>外，还支持以下属性：</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 926px;">     <h3 id="title" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">title<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="title" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>title(value: ResourceStr | CustomBuilder | NavigationCommonTitle | NavigationCustomTitle, options?: NavigationTitleOptions)</p>     <p>设置页面标题。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a><sup>10+</sup> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a> | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationcommontitle9">NavigationCommonTitle</a><sup>9+</sup> | <a    <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">页面标题，使用NavigationCustomTitle类型设置height高度时，<a </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 633px;">     <h3 id="menus" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">menus<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="menus" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>menus(value: Array&lt;NavigationMenuItem&gt; | CustomBuilder)</p>     <p>设置页面右上角菜单。不设置时不显示菜单项。使用Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmenuitem">NavigationMenuItem</a>&gt; 写法时，竖屏最多支持显示3个图标，横屏最多支持显示5个图标，多余的图标会被放入自动生成的更多图标。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>不支持通过SymbolGlyphModifier对象的fontSize属性修改图标大小、effectStrategy属性修改动效、symbolEffect属性修改动效类型。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmenuitem">NavigationMenuItem</a>&gt; | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">页面右上角菜单。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 702px;">     <h3 id="menus19" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">menus<sup>19+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="menus19" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>menus(items: Array&lt;NavigationMenuItem&gt; | CustomBuilder, options?: NavigationMenuOptions)</p>     <p>设置页面右上角菜单。不设置时不显示菜单项。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#menus">menus</a>相比，新增菜单选项。使用Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmenuitem">NavigationMenuItem</a>&gt; 写法时，竖屏最多支持显示3个图标，横屏最多支持显示5个图标，多余的图标会被放入自动生成的更多图标。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>       <p>不支持通过SymbolGlyphModifier对象的fontSize属性修改图标大小、effectStrategy属性修改动效、symbolEffect属性修改动效类型。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">items</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">页面右上角菜单选项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="titlemode" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">titleMode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="titlemode" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span CustomBuilder, options?: NavigationToolbarOptions)</p>     <p>设置工具栏内容。不设置时不显示工具栏。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 20开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>       <p>不支持通过SymbolGlyphModifier对象的fontSize属性修改图标大小、effectStrategy属性修改动效、symbolEffect属性修改动效类型。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>工具栏内容，使用Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#toolbaritem10">ToolbarItem</a>&gt;写法设置的工具栏有如下特性：</p>          <p>工具栏所有选项均分底部工具栏，在每个均分内容区布局文本和图标。</p>          <p>竖屏最多支持显示5个图标，多余的图标会被放入自动生成的更多图标。横屏时，如果为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmode9枚举说明">Split</a>模式，仍按照竖屏规则显示，如果为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmode9枚举说明">Stack</a>模式需配合menus属性的Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmenuitem">NavigationMenuItem</a>&gt;使用，底部工具栏会自动隐藏，同时底部工具栏所有选项移动至页面右上角菜单。</p>          <p>使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a>写法为用户自定义工具栏选项，除均分底部工具栏外不具备以上功能。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">工具栏选项。 包含工具栏背景颜色、工具栏背景模糊样式及模糊选项、工具栏背景属性、工具栏布局方式、是否隐藏工具栏的文本、工具栏更多图标的菜单选项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div> <p>创建NavDestination组件。使用builder函数，基于name和param构造NavDestination组件。builder下只能有一个根节点。builder中允许在NavDestination组件外包含一层自定义组件， 但自定义组件不允许设置属性和事件，否则仅显示空白。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 661px;">     <h3 id="navbarwidthrange10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">navBarWidthRange<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>navBarWidthRange(value: [Dimension, Dimension])</p>     <p>设置导航栏最小和最大宽度（双栏模式下生效）。</p>     <p><strong>规则：</strong> 优先级规则详见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#mincontentwidth10">minContentWidth</a>说明。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">[<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#dimension10">Dimension</a>]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 961px;">     <h3 id="mincontentwidth10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">minContentWidth<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="mincontentwidth10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>minContentWidth(value: Dimension)</p>     <p>设置导航栏内容区最小宽度（双栏模式下生效）。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>优先级规则：</p>       <ol>        <li>         <p>仅设置navBarWidth，不支持Navigation分割线拖拽。</p></li>        <li>         <p>navBarWidthRange指定分割线可以拖拽范围。如果不设置值，则按照默认值处理。拖拽范围需要满足navBarWidthRange设置的范围和minContentWidth限制。</p></li>        <li>         <p>Navigation显示范围缩小：a. 缩小内容区大小。如果不设置minContentWidth属性，则可以缩小内容区至0， 否则最小缩小至minContentWidth。b. 缩小导航栏大小，缩小时需要满足导航栏宽度大于navBarRange的下限。c. 对显示内容进行裁切。</p></li>       </ol>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#dimension10">Dimension</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>导航栏内容区最小宽度。</p>          <p>默认值：360</p>          <p>单位：vp</p>          <p>undefined：行为不做处理，导航栏内容区最小宽度与默认值保持一致。</p>          <p>Auto模式断点计算：默认600vp，minNavBarWidth(240vp) + minContentWidth (360vp)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h3 id="ignorelayoutsafearea12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">ignoreLayoutSafeArea<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ignorelayoutsafearea12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>ignoreLayoutSafeArea(types?: Array&lt;LayoutSafeAreaType&gt;, edges?: Array&lt;LayoutSafeAreaEdge&gt;)</p>     <p>控制组件的布局，使其扩展到非安全区域。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>组件设置ignoreLayoutSafeArea之后生效的条件为：</p>       <p>设置LayoutSafeAreaType.SYSTEM时，组件的边界与非安全区域重合时组件能够延伸到非安全区域下。例如：设备顶部状态栏高度100，组件在屏幕中纵向方位的绝对偏移需要在0到100之间。</p>       <p>若组件延伸到非安全区域内，此时在非安全区域里触发的事件（例如：点击事件）等可能会被系统拦截，优先响应状态栏等系统组件。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">types</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array &lt;<a </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 937px;">     <h3 id="systembarstyle12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">systemBarStyle<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="systembarstyle12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>systemBarStyle(style: Optional&lt;SystemBarStyle&gt;)</p>     <p>当Navigation中显示Navigation首页时，设置对应系统状态栏的样式。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ol>        <li>不建议混合使用systemBarStyle属性和window设置状态栏样式的相关接口，例如：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-window-window#setwindowsystembarproperties9">setWindowSystemBarProperties</a>。</li>        <li>初次设置Navigation/NavDestination的systemBarStyle属性时，会备份当前状态栏样式用于后续的恢复场景。</li>        <li>Navigation总是以首页（路由栈内没有NavDestination时）或者栈顶NavDestination设置的状态栏样式为准。</li>        <li>Navigation首页或者任何栈顶NavDestination页面，如果设置了有效的systemBarStyle，则会使用设置的样式，反之如果之前已经备份了样式，则使用备份的样式，否则不做任何处理。</li>        <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navigationmode9枚举说明">Split</a>模式下的Navigation，如果内容区没有NavDestination，则遵从Navigation首页的设置，反之则遵从栈顶NavDestination的设置。</li>        <li>仅支持在主窗口的主页面中使用systemBarStyle设置状态栏样式。</li>        <li>仅当Navigation占满整个页面时，设置的样式才会生效，当Navigation没有占满整个页面时，如果有备份的样式，则恢复备份的样式。</li>        <li>当页面设置不同样式时，在页面转场开始时生效。</li>        <li>非全屏窗口下，Navigation/NavDestination设置的状态栏不生效。</li>       </ol>       <p>从API version 20开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">style</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-custom-property#optionalt12">Optional</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-window-i#systembarstyle12">SystemBarStyle</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">系统状态栏样式。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 777px;">     <h3 id="recoverable14" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">recoverable<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="recoverable14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>recoverable(recoverable: Optional&lt;boolean&gt;)</p>     <p>配置Navigation是否可恢复。如配置为可恢复，当应用进程异常退出并重新冷启动时，可自动创建该Navigation，并恢复至异常退出时的路由栈。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ol>        <li>使用该接口需要先设置Navigation的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-component-id#id">id属性</a>，否则该接口无效。</li>        <li>该接口需要配合NavDestination的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navdestination#recoverable14">recoverable</a>接口使用。</li>        <li>恢复的过程中不可序列化的信息，例如不可序列化的参数与用户设置的onPop等，会被丢弃，无法恢复。</li>        <li>当应用退到后台，因系统资源不足等原因被系统终止后，如果某页面已配置为可恢复，当应用再次被唤醒至前台时，系统将自动恢复该页面。详细说明请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/ability-recover-guideline" target="_blank">UIAbility备份恢复</a>，详细使用请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#示例18设置navigation可恢复">示例18</a>。</li>       </ol>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">recoverable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-custom-property#optionalt12">Optional</a>&lt;boolean&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Navigation是否可恢复，默认为不可恢复。</p>          <p>默认值：false。</p>          <p>true：路由栈可恢复。</p>          <p>false：路由栈不可恢复。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 565px;">     <h3 id="enabledragbar14" href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navdestination#onshown10">onShown</a>生命周期与全模态的联动触发。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version <p>true：全模态拉起时，会触发当前NavDestination页面的onHidden生命周期；全模态关闭时会触发当前NavDestination页面的onShown生命周期</p>          <p>false：NavDestination页面onHidden、onShown生命周期不会因为全模态的拉起、关闭而触发。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 469px;">     <h3 id="subtitledeprecated" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 538px;">     <h2 id="navpathstack10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">NavPathStack<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navpathstack10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Navigation导航控制器，以栈的数据结构管理Navigation中所有的子页面，并提供栈操作的方法用于控制Navigation中子页面的切换。</p>     <p>从API version 12开始，NavPathStack允许被继承，派生类对象可以替代基类NavPathStack对象使用。使用示例参见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#示例10定义导航控制器派生类">示例10</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>1.连续调用多个导航控制器操作方法时，中间过程会被忽略，显示最终的栈操作结果。</p>       <p>例如：在Page1页面先pop再push一个Page1，系统会认为操作前和操作后的结果一致而不进行任何操作，如果需要强行push一个Page1实例，可以使用NEW_INSTANCE模式。</p>       <p>2.不建议开发者通过监听生命周期的方式管理自己的导航控制器。</p>       <p>3.在应用处于后台状态下，调用NavPathStack的栈操作方法，会在应用再次回到前台状态时触发刷新。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 302px;">     <h3 id="constructor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">constructor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="constructor" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>constructor()</p>     <p>创建NavPathStack对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 610px;">     <h3 id="pushpath10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">pushPath<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="pushpath10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>pushPath(info: NavPathInfo, animated?: boolean): void</p>     <p>将info指定的NavDestination页面信息入栈。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">info</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathinfo10">NavPathInfo</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">pop<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="pop10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>pop(animated?: boolean): NavPathInfo | undefined</p>     <p>弹出路由栈栈顶元素。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>连续调用多个导航控制器方法时，中间被pop的页面会被缓存，后续push同名页面时会优先复用该页面，不会走新的页面创建流程。</p>       <p>例如：</p>       <p>pathStack: NavPathStack = new NavPathStack()</p>       <p>// 初始页面栈为：[A]</p>       <p>pathStack.pop()</p>       <p>pathStack.pushPath(A)</p>       <p>pathStack.pushPath(B)</p>       <p>// 操作后页面栈为：[A B]</p>       <p>此时A页面会被复用，不会走新的创建流程。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">animated<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否支持转场动画，</p>          <p>默认值：true。</p>          <p>true：支持转场动画。</p>          <p>false：不支持转场动画。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th <p>NavPathInfo：返回栈顶NavDestination页面的信息。</p>          <p>undefined: 当路由栈为空时返回undefined。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" null</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果当前NavPathStack所属Navigation的外层有另外的一层Navigation，则能够获取到外层Navigation的NavPathStack。否则获取不到NavPathStack，返回null。</td>        </tr>        </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 934px;">     <h3 id="setpathstack19" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setPathStack<sup>19+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setpathstack19" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setPathStack(pathStack: Array&lt;NavPathInfo&gt;, animated?: boolean): void</p>     <p>将当前路由栈中的路由页面信息数组更新为指定内容，并实现路由转场。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.78.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">pathStack</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathinfo10">NavPathInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置当前路由栈中的路由页面信息数组。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>数组长度无限制。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">animated</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否开启转场动画。</p>          <p>默认值：true。</p>          <p>true：开启转场动画。</p>          <p>false：不开启转场动画。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ol>        <li>开发者可以在原有栈的基础上批量添加或删除页面。批量入栈的页面中，只有可见的页面会触发创建，其他页面虽已入栈但不会立即创建，当这些页面变为可见时，才会触发创建。</li>        <li>通过批量入栈功能更新的路由栈，各页面的生命周期事件触发顺序为从栈顶到底部依次触发，这与其它入栈接口从栈底到顶部的触发顺序不同。</li>        <li>开发者可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navpathinfo10">NavPathInfo</a>中的页面唯一标识符navDestinationId来操作已有页面，该id由系统默认生成且全局唯一（可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#getpathstack19">getPathStack</a>接口获取，不可主动赋新值）。若该id在当前路由栈中不存在，则表示新增页面，若在当前路由栈中存在，同时对应的name相同，则表示复用已有页面。</li>       </ol>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="navpathinfo10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">constructor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>constructor(name: string, param: unknown, onPop?: Callback&lt;PopInfo&gt;, isEntry?: boolean)</p>     <p>创建NavPathInfo对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.80.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.80.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.80.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.80.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">name</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>NavDestination页面名称。该名称匹配开发者设置的路由表中的name，包括以下两种：</p>          <p>1. 自定义路由表，开发者通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#navdestination10">navDestination</a>方法传递。</p>          <p>2. 系统路由表，通过routerMap中的name设置，可参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#示例2使用导航控制器方法">示例2</a>。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">param</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">unknown</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">开发者设置的NavDestination页面详细参数，unknown可以是用户自定义的类型。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">onPop<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#popinfo11">PopInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">NavDestination页面触发<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#pop11">pop</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#poptoname11">popToName</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#poptoindex11">popToIndex</a>时返回的回调。仅<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#pop11">pop</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#poptoname11">popToName</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-navigation#poptoindex11">popToIndex</a>中设置result参数后触发。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isEntry<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>标记NavDestination是否为入口页面。</p>          <p>默认值：false。</p>          <p>true：NavDestination是入口页面。</p>          <p>false：NavDestination不是入口页面。</p>          <p>标记清理时机：1. 在当前navDestination页面触发一次全局返回事件。2. 应用退至后台。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>入口NavDestination不响应应用内的全局back事件，直接触发应用间的全局back事件。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2089px;">     <h3 id="属性-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">isEntry<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" <p>true：NavDestination是入口页面。</p>          <p>false：NavDestination不是入口页面。</p>          <p>标记清理时机：1. 在当前navDestination页面触发一次全局back事件。2. 应用退至后台。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>入口NavDestination不响应应用内的全局back事件，直接触发应用间的全局back事件。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder"    <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NORMAL</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder"   <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置工具栏单个选项为DISABLED态， 该选项显示DISABLED态样式，并且不可交互。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ACTIVE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">设置工具栏单个选项为ACTIVE态， 该选项通过点击事件可以将icon图标更新为activeIcon对应的图片资源。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1023px;">     <h2 id="navigationtitlemode枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">NavigationTitleMode枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navigationtitlemode枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>标题栏显示模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Free</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>当内容为满一屏的可滚动组件时，标题随着内容向上滚动而缩小（子标题的大小不变、淡出）。向下滚动内容到顶时则恢复原样。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>标题随着内容滚动大小联动的动效在title设置为ResourceStr和NavigationCommonTitle时生效，设置成其余自定义节点类型时字体样式无法变化，下拉时只影响标题栏偏移。</p>          <p>可滚动组件不满一屏时，如果想使用联动效果，就要使用滚动组件提供的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-list#edgeeffect">edgeEffect</a>接口将options参数设置为true。未滚动状态，标题栏高度与Full模式一致；滚动时，标题栏的最小高度与Mini模式一致。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Full</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>固定为大标题模式。</p>          <p>默认值：只有主标题时，标题栏高度为112vp；同时有主标题和副标题时，标题栏高度为138vp。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Mini</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>固定为小标题模式。</p>          <p>默认值：API version 12之前，只有主标题时，标题栏高度为56vp；同时有主标题和副标题时，标题栏高度为82vp。从API version 12开始，该模式下标题栏高度为56vp。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 456px;">     <h2 id="navbarposition9枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">NavBarPosition<sup>9+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.100.5.1.3.1.1" width="50%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.100.5.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Start</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">双栏显示时，主列在主轴方向首部。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1656px;">     <h2 id="navigationmode9枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">NavigationMode<sup>9+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navigationmode9枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>导航栏显示模式。Navigation处于分栏显示状态时，导航栏和内容区之间会显示分割线。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Stack</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">导航栏与内容区独立显示，相当于两个页面。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Split</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>导航栏与内容区分两栏显示。</p>          <p><strong>1.</strong> navBarWidth最终取值与开发者设置值的关系参见表1。</p>          <p><strong>2.</strong> 缩小组件尺寸时，先缩小内容区的尺寸至minContentWidth，然后再缩小导航栏的尺寸至minNavBarWidth。若继续缩小，先缩小内容区，内容区消失后再缩小导航栏。</p>          <p><strong>3.</strong> 设置导航栏为固定尺寸时，若持续缩小组件尺寸，导航栏最后压缩显示。</p>          <p><strong>4.</strong> 若只设置了navBarWidth属性，则导航栏宽度为navBarWidth，且分割线不可拖动。</p>          <p><strong>5.</strong> 分割线的热区左右各2vp，建议避让4vp以上。</p>          <p><strong>6.</strong> Split模式下，内容区若只存在一个页面，则页面左上角不会显示返回按钮。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Auto</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>API version 9之前：窗口宽度&gt;=520vp时，采用Split模式显示；窗口宽度&lt;520vp时，采用Stack模式显示。</p>          <p>API version 10及以上：窗口宽度&gt;=600vp时，采用Split模式显示；窗口宽度&lt;600vp时，采用Stack模式显示，600vp等于minNavBarWidth(240vp) + minContentWidth (360vp)。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>表1</strong> navBarWidth最终取值与开发者设置值的关系表</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">开发者设置的navBarWidth值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth计算值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">navBarWidth最终取值</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">navBarWidth &lt; minNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NA</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">navBarWidth &gt; maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth &gt; maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">maxNavBarWidth</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">navBarWidth &gt; maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth &lt; minNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">navBarWidth &gt; maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth ≤ calcNavBarWidth ≤ maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth ≤ navBarWidth ≤ maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth ≤ minNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth ≤ navBarWidth ≤ maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth &lt; calcNavBarWidth &lt;= navBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">minNavBarWidth ≤ navBarWidth ≤ maxNavBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">calcNavBarWidth &gt; navBarWidth</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">navBarWidth</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>为了简化表示，可以将组件宽度 - minContentWidth - 分割线宽度 (1vp)称为calcNavBarWidth。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 471px;">     <h2 id="navigationoperation11枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">NavigationOperation<sup>11+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"  <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">POP</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 663px;">     <h2 id="barstyle12枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">BarStyle<sup>12+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="barstyle12枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>标题栏或工具栏的布局样式。NavDestination的工具栏不支持设置该属性。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.103.4.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.103.4.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" width="33.33333333333333%">STANDARD</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>指定该模式的标题栏或工具栏与内容区采用上下布局。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" <p>指定该模式的标题栏或工具栏与内容区采用层叠布局，标题栏或工具栏布局在内容区上层。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder"   <p>将指定该模式的标题栏或工具栏设置为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#safeareapadding14">组件级安全区</a>。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>          <p>系统默认的栈操作模式。</p>          <p>push操作会将指定的NavDestination入栈；replace操作会将当前栈顶NavDestination替换。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">MOVE_TO_TOP_SINGLETON</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">从栈底向栈顶查找，如果指定的名称已经存在，则将对应的NavDestination页面移到栈顶（replace操作会将最后的栈顶替换成指定的NavDestination），否则行为和STANDARD一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">POP_TO_SINGLETON</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">从栈底向栈顶查找，如果指定的名称已经存在，则将其上方的NavDestination页面全部移除（replace操作会将最后的栈顶替换成指定的NavDestination），否则行为和STANDARD一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NEW_INSTANCE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">3</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">创建新的NavDestination实例。与STANDARD模式相比，该方法不会复用栈中同名实例。并且指定该模式时，新创建的页面默认会执行push动效。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 594px;">     <h2 id="navigationoptions12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">NavigationOptions<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="navigationoptions12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span auto 3058px;">     <h3 id="示例1navigation页面布局" class="firsth2">示例1（Navigation页面布局）<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例1navigation页面布局" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3> anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例18设置navigation可恢复" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>该示例演示如何使用<a class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-iri-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-iri-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-iri-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iri-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="json prettyprint linenums hljs language-json" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-punctuation">{</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">"routerMap"</span><span class="hljs-punctuation">:</span> <span class="hljs-punctuation">[</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-punctuation">{</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-attr">"name"</span><span class="hljs-punctuation">:</span> <span class="hljs-punctuation">}</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>为模拟进程异常退出并重新冷启动，可执行以下步骤：</p>       <ol>        <li>         <p>工程运行成功后点击跳转按钮。</p></li>        <li>         <p>应用上划回退到后台，开启命令行窗口。</p></li>        <li>         <p>输入"hdc shell"，回车后输入"pidof 工程包名"，查询pid值。</p></li>        <li>         <p>输入"aa force-stop 工程包名 -p pid值 -r RESOURCE_CONTROL"进行回车，模拟资源使用不当导致的应用退出。</p></li>        <li>         <p>点击应用重新进入，可发现页面依然是点击跳转按钮后的页面。</p></li>       </ol>      </div></div></div>     <p><span><img originheight="804" originwidth="388" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115436.70082117493571649460260187648304:50001231000000:2800:4E1CB8A808509E1B301EA11F8EAD8B93ECEC6EE0AC69823644D74BC2B96527B5.gif"
